### [289] [Revisiting the Bertrand Paradox via Equilibrium Analysis of No-regret Learners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21620)
*Arnab Maiti,Junyan Liu,Kevin Jamieson,Lillian J. Ratliff*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究离散Bertrand定价博弈，分析无遗憾学习者在重复博弈中如何影响价格均衡，探讨Bertrand悖论（理论预测低价但现实市场维持高价）的成因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bertrand悖论指出经典理论预测低价竞争，但现实市场常维持高价。本文旨在通过分析无遗憾学习者在重复博弈中的行为，解释理论与现实的差距。

Method: 采用离散Bertrand定价博弈模型，n≥2个玩家从集合{1/k, 2/k, ..., 1}中同时选择价格。研究重复博弈中玩家使用无遗憾学习算法（包括无外部遗憾和无交换遗憾）时的均衡结果。

Result: 理论分析表明无外部遗憾学习者可能收敛到不理想的高价结果，而更强的无交换遗憾保证则能促进竞争性低价行为的出现。实验支持理论并揭示无交换遗憾学习者的意外现象。

Conclusion: 无遗憾学习保证的类型显著影响Bertrand博弈的均衡结果：无外部遗憾可能导致高价均衡，而无交换遗憾则更可能实现竞争性低价，这有助于解释Bertrand悖论。

Abstract: We study the discrete Bertrand pricing game with a non-increasing demand function. The game has $n \ge 2$ players who simultaneously choose prices from the set $\{1/k, 2/k, \ldots, 1\}$, where $k\in\mathbb{N}$. The player who sets the lowest price captures the entire demand; if multiple players tie for the lowest price, they split the demand equally.
  We study the Bertrand paradox, where classical theory predicts low prices, yet real markets often sustain high prices. To understand this gap, we analyze a repeated-game model in which firms set prices using no-regret learners. Our goal is to characterize the equilibrium outcomes that can arise under different no-regret learning guarantees. We are particularly interested in questions such as whether no-external-regret learners can converge to undesirable high-price outcomes, and how stronger guarantees such as no-swap regret shape the emergence of competitive low-price behavior. We address these and related questions through a theoretical analysis, complemented by experiments that support the theory and reveal surprising phenomena for no-swap regret learners.

</details>


### [290] [Solving Imperfect-Recall Games via Sum-of-Squares Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21722)
*Rui Zheng,Ryann Sim,Antonios Varvitsiotis*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 该论文针对不完全回忆扩展式博弈提出基于平方和层次的方法，用于计算单人和多人博弈中的最优策略和纳什均衡，证明了方法的收敛性并识别了特殊类别使计算简化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展式博弈是建模序列决策的强大框架，但现有算法大多假设完全回忆。现实中玩家可能忘记历史信息，形成不完全回忆博弈，其均衡计算被证明是困难的，需要新的计算方法。

Method: 提出平方和层次方法，在行为策略空间上计算单人不完全回忆博弈的最优策略和多人博弈的纳什均衡。该方法将博弈优化问题转化为一系列半定规划。

Result: 理论证明显示：(1) 平方和层次渐近收敛；(2) 在一般性假设下收敛是有限的；(3) 在单人不心不在焉博弈中，收敛发生在由信息集数量决定的有限层次。还识别了(SOS)-凹和(SOS)-单调博弈类别，使单层SDP即可计算均衡。

Conclusion: 平方和层次为不完全回忆扩展式博弈提供了有效的计算方法，在理论和计算上都有良好性质，特别是对于特殊类别的博弈可以高效求解，为解决这一困难问题提供了新途径。

Abstract: Extensive-form games (EFGs) provide a powerful framework for modeling sequential decision making, capturing strategic interaction under imperfect information, chance events, and temporal structure. Most positive algorithmic and theoretical results for EFGs assume perfect recall, where players remember all past information and actions. We study the increasingly relevant setting of imperfect-recall EFGs (IREFGs), where players may forget parts of their history or previously acquired information, and where equilibrium computation is provably hard. We propose sum-of-squares (SOS) hierarchies for computing ex-ante optimal strategies in single-player IREFGs and Nash equilibria in multi-player IREFGs, working over behavioral strategies. Our theoretical results show that (i) these hierarchies converge asymptotically, (ii) under genericity assumptions, the convergence is finite, and (iii) in single-player non-absentminded IREFGs, convergence occurs at a finite level determined by the number of information sets. Finally, we introduce the new classes of (SOS)-concave and (SOS)-monotone IREFGs, and show that in the single-player setting the SOS hierarchy converges at the first level, enabling equilibrium computation with a single semidefinite program (SDP).

</details>


### [291] [Autobidding Equilibria in Sponsored Shopping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.21966)
*Paul Dütting,Renato Paes Leme,Yuhao Li,Kelly Spendlove,Yifeng Teng*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究数字市场中赞助购物拍卖的自动竞价均衡与效率损失，证明了GSP和VCG机制都存在均衡且价格无政府状态比为2


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着商业向数字市场转移，平台通过赞助购物拍卖变现流量。与传统的"赞助搜索"不同，广告主拥有多样化的产品目录，可以在同一查询中同时获得多个广告位，这带来了组合分配的复杂性。

Method: 研究自动竞价场景，价值最大化代理采用统一竞价策略，在投资回报率约束下优化总价值。分析两种主流拍卖格式：广义第二价格(GSP)和维克里-克拉克-格罗夫斯(VCG)机制。

Result: 1. 证明了两种设置下都存在自动竞价均衡；2. 证明了两种机制的价格无政府状态比(PoA)都为2，且这个界限是紧的。

Conclusion: 赞助购物拍卖中的组合分配问题在自动竞价环境下存在均衡解，GSP和VCG机制都能达到相同的效率界限，为平台设计提供了理论依据。

Abstract: As commerce shifts to digital marketplaces, platforms increasingly monetize traffic through Sponsored Shopping auctions. Unlike classic ``Sponsored Search", where an advertiser typically bids for a single link, these settings involve advertisers with broad catalogs of distinct products. In these auctions, a single advertiser can secure multiple slots simultaneously to promote different items within the same query. This creates a fundamental complexity: the allocation is combinatorial, as advertisers simultaneously win a bundle of slots rather than a single position.
  We study this setting through the lens of autobidding, where value-maximizing agents employ uniform bidding strategies to optimize total value subject to Return-on-Investment (ROI) constraints. We analyze two prevalent auction formats: Generalized Second-Price (GSP) and Vickrey-Clarke-Groves (VCG). Our first main contribution is establishing the universal existence of an Autobidding Equilibrium for both settings. Second, we prove a tight Price of Anarchy (PoA) of 2 for both mechanisms.

### [292] [Timing Games: Probabilistic backrunning and spam](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.22032)
*Bruno Mazorra,Christoph Schlegel,Akaki Mamageishvili*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究玩家在机会出现后最快行动的游戏，应用于区块链中的"概率性后跑"问题，分析对称均衡和效率损失


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究区块链中的"概率性后跑"现象，即套利者试图在影响价格交易或预言机更新后立即下单，这种竞争会产生昂贵的"垃圾"交易

Method: 建立玩家竞争时机的博弈模型，机会随机出现在时间区间，玩家只能延迟观察到机会出现，行动有成本，分析对称均衡

Result: 描述了该博弈的唯一对称均衡，并研究了均衡的最坏情况效率损失

Conclusion: 该模型为分析区块链中的后跑竞争提供了理论框架，行动次数可解释为竞争机会产生的昂贵"垃圾"交易成本

Abstract: There are $n$ players who compete by timing their actions. An opportunity appears randomly on a time interval. Whoever takes an action the fastest after the opportunity has arisen wins. The occurrence of the opportunity is observed only with a delay. Taking actions is costly. We characterize the unique symmetric equilibrium of this game and study worst-case inefficiency of equilibria. Our main motivation is the study of ``probabilistic backrunning" on blockchains, where arbitrageurs want to place an order immediately after a trade that impacts the price on an exchange or after an oracle update. In this context, the number of actions taken can be interpreted as a measure of costly ``spam" generated to compete for the opportunity.

</details>
